1	1	Extract data for BillControl	1	SELECT 
REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(BillControl.ClientCode, '|', ' '), CHAR(13), ' '),  CHAR(10), ' '), 
BillControl.BillSeq, 
BillControl.BillControlSeq, 
BillControl.ModDate, 
BillControl.CreateDate, 
REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(BillControl.Control, '|', ' '), CHAR(13), ' '),  CHAR(10), ' '), 
REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(BillControl.ExternalID, '|', ' '), CHAR(13), ' '),  CHAR(10), ' '), 
BillControl.BatchNumber, 
REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(BillControl.ModUserID, '|', ' '), CHAR(13), ' '),  CHAR(10), ' '), 
REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(BillControl.ExternalID2, '|', ' '), CHAR(13), ' '),  CHAR(10), ' '), 
NULL AS Message,
'I'
FROM ~SNAPSHOT~.dbo.BillControl	SELECT 
REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(ct.ClientCode, '|', ' '), CHAR(13), ' '),  CHAR(10), ' '), 
ct.BillSeq, 
ct.BillControlSeq, 
BillControl.ModDate, 
BillControl.CreateDate, 
REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(BillControl.Control, '|', ' '), CHAR(13), ' '),  CHAR(10), ' '), 
REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(BillControl.ExternalID, '|', ' '), CHAR(13), ' '),  CHAR(10), ' '), 
BillControl.BatchNumber, 
REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(BillControl.ModUserID, '|', ' '), CHAR(13), ' '),  CHAR(10), ' '), 
REPLACE(REPLACE(REPLACE(BillControl.ExternalID2, '|', ' '), CHAR(13), ' '),  CHAR(10), ' '), 
NULL AS Message,
ct.SYS_CHANGE_OPERATION
FROM ~SNAPSHOT~.dbo.BillControl
RIGHT OUTER JOIN CHANGETABLE (CHANGES ~SNAPSHOT~.dbo.BillControl, ~PREVIOUSCTVERSION~) AS ct ON BillControl.BillControlSeq=ct.BillControlSeq
AND BillControl.BillSeq=ct.BillSeq
AND BillControl.ClientCode=ct.ClientCode	8.08
